30 static bool useCompactUnwind(const Triple &T) { 0
31 // Only on darwin. ----
32 if (!T.isOSDarwin()) 0
33 return false; 0
34 ----
35 // aarch64 always has it. ----
36 if (T.getArch() == Triple::aarch64 || T.getArch() == Triple::aarch64_32) 0
37 return true; 0
38 ----
39 // armv7k always has it. ----
40 if (T.isWatchABI()) 0
41 return true; 0
42 ----
43 // Use it on newer version of OS X. ----
44 if (T.isMacOSX() && !T.isMacOSXVersionLT(10, 6)) 0
45 return true; 0
46 ----
47 // And the iOS simulator. ----
48 if (T.isiOS() && T.isX86()) 0
49 return true; 0
50 ----
51 // The rest of the simulators always have it. ----
52 if (T.isSimulatorEnvironment()) 0
53 return true; 0
54 ----
55 return false; 0
56 } ----

542 void MCObjectFileInfo::initGOFFMCObjectFileInfo(const Triple &T) { 0
543 TextSection = 0
544 Ctx->getGOFFSection(".text", SectionKind::getText(), nullptr, nullptr); 0
545 BSSSection = 0
546 Ctx->getGOFFSection(".bss", SectionKind::getBSS(), nullptr, nullptr); 0
547 PPA1Section = 0
548 Ctx->getGOFFSection(".ppa1", SectionKind::getMetadata(), TextSection, 0
549 MCConstantExpr::create(GOFF::SK_PPA1, *Ctx)); 0
550 ADASection = 0
551 Ctx->getGOFFSection(".ada", SectionKind::getData(), nullptr, nullptr); 0
552 } 0
553 ----
554 void MCObjectFileInfo::initCOFFMCObjectFileInfo(const Triple &T) { 0
555 EHFrameSection = 0
556 Ctx->getCOFFSection(".eh_frame", COFF::IMAGE_SCN_CNT_INITIALIZED_DATA | 0
557 COFF::IMAGE_SCN_MEM_READ, ----
558 SectionKind::getData()); ----
559 ----
560 // Set the `IMAGE_SCN_MEM_16BIT` flag when compiling for thumb mode. This is ----
561 // used to indicate to the linker that the text segment contains thumb instructions ----
562 // and to set the ISA selection bit for calls accordingly. ----
563 const bool IsThumb = T.getArch() == Triple::thumb; 0
564 ----
565 // COFF ----
566 BSSSection = Ctx->getCOFFSection( 0
567 ".bss", COFF::IMAGE_SCN_CNT_UNINITIALIZED_DATA | ----
568 COFF::IMAGE_SCN_MEM_READ | COFF::IMAGE_SCN_MEM_WRITE, ----
569 SectionKind::getBSS()); ----
570 TextSection = Ctx->getCOFFSection( 0
571 ".text", ----
572 (IsThumb ? COFF::IMAGE_SCN_MEM_16BIT : (COFF::SectionCharacteristics)0) | ----
573 COFF::IMAGE_SCN_CNT_CODE | COFF::IMAGE_SCN_MEM_EXECUTE | ----
574 COFF::IMAGE_SCN_MEM_READ, ----
575 SectionKind::getText()); ----
576 DataSection = Ctx->getCOFFSection( 0
577 ".data", COFF::IMAGE_SCN_CNT_INITIALIZED_DATA | COFF::IMAGE_SCN_MEM_READ | ----
578 COFF::IMAGE_SCN_MEM_WRITE, ----
579 SectionKind::getData()); ----
580 ReadOnlySection = Ctx->getCOFFSection( 0
581 ".rdata", COFF::IMAGE_SCN_CNT_INITIALIZED_DATA | COFF::IMAGE_SCN_MEM_READ, ----
582 SectionKind::getReadOnly()); ----
583 ----
584 if (T.getArch() == Triple::x86_64 || T.getArch() == Triple::aarch64 || 0
585 T.getArch() == Triple::arm || T.getArch() == Triple::thumb) { 0

587 LSDASection = nullptr; 0

926 // The default csect for program code. Functions without a specified section ----

929 // name being empty (considering named symbols to be "user symbol names"). ----

1092 MCSection *MCObjectFileInfo::getDwarfComdatSection(const char *Name, 0
1093 uint64_t Hash) const { ----
1094 switch (Ctx->getTargetTriple().getObjectFormat()) { 0
1095 case Triple::ELF: 0
1096 return Ctx->getELFSection(Name, ELF::SHT_PROGBITS, ELF::SHF_GROUP, 0, 0
1097 utostr(Hash), /*IsComdat=*/true); 0
1098 case Triple::Wasm: 0
1099 return Ctx->getWasmSection(Name, SectionKind::getMetadata(), 0, 0
1100 utostr(Hash), MCContext::GenericSectionID); 0
1101 case Triple::MachO: 0
1102 case Triple::COFF: ----
1103 case Triple::GOFF: ----
1104 case Triple::SPIRV: ----
1105 case Triple::XCOFF: ----
1106 case Triple::DXContainer: ----
1107 case Triple::UnknownObjectFormat: ----
1108 report_fatal_error("Cannot get DWARF comdat section for this object file " 0
1109 "format: not implemented."); ----
1110 break; ----
1111 } ----
1112 llvm_unreachable("Unknown ObjectFormatType"); 0
1113 } ----

1116 MCObjectFileInfo::getStackSizesSection(const MCSection &TextSec) const { 0
1117 if ((Ctx->getObjectFileType() != MCContext::IsELF) || 0
1118 Ctx->getTargetTriple().isPS4()) 0
1119 return StackSizesSection; 0
1120 ----
1121 const MCSectionELF &ElfSec = static_cast(TextSec); 0
1122 unsigned Flags = ELF::SHF_LINK_ORDER; 0
1123 StringRef GroupName; 0
1124 if (const MCSymbol *Group = ElfSec.getGroup()) { 0
1125 GroupName = Group->getName(); 0
1126 Flags |= ELF::SHF_GROUP; 0
1127 } ----
1128 ----
1129 return Ctx->getELFSection(".stack_sizes", ELF::SHT_PROGBITS, Flags, 0, 0
1130 GroupName, true, ElfSec.getUniqueID(), ----
1131 cast(TextSec.getBeginSymbol())); 0

1191 MCSection * ----
1192 MCObjectFileInfo::getPseudoProbeDescSection(StringRef FuncName) const { 0
1193 if (Ctx->getObjectFileType() == MCContext::IsELF) { 0
1194 // Create a separate comdat group for each function's descriptor in order ----
1195 // for the linker to deduplicate. The duplication, must be from different ----
1196 // tranlation unit, can come from: ----
1197 // 1. Inline functions defined in header files; ----
1198 // 2. ThinLTO imported funcions; ----
1199 // 3. Weak-linkage definitions. ----
1200 // Use a concatenation of the section name and the function name as the ----
1201 // group name so that descriptor-only groups won't be folded with groups of ----
1202 // code. ----
1203 if (Ctx->getTargetTriple().supportsCOMDAT() && !FuncName.empty()) { 0
1204 auto *S = static_cast(PseudoProbeDescSection); 0
1205 auto Flags = S->getFlags() | ELF::SHF_GROUP; 0
1206 return Ctx->getELFSection(S->getName(), S->getType(), Flags, 0
1207 S->getEntrySize(), ----
1208 S->getName() + "_" + FuncName, 0
1209 /*IsComdat=*/true); 0
1210 } ----
1211 } ----
1212 return PseudoProbeDescSection; 0
1213 } ----

1216 return LLVMStatsSection; 0
1217 } ----
1218 ----
1219 MCSection *MCObjectFileInfo::getPCSection(StringRef Name, 0
1220 const MCSection *TextSec) const { ----
1221 if (Ctx->getObjectFileType() != MCContext::IsELF) 0
1222 return nullptr; 0
1223 ----
1224 // SHF_WRITE for relocations, and let user post-process data in-place. ----
1225 unsigned Flags = ELF::SHF_WRITE | ELF::SHF_ALLOC | ELF::SHF_LINK_ORDER; 0
1226 ----
1227 if (!TextSec) 0
1228 TextSec = getTextSection(); 0
1229 ----
1230 StringRef GroupName; 0
1231 const auto &ElfSec = static_cast(*TextSec); 0
1232 if (const MCSymbol *Group = ElfSec.getGroup()) { 0
1233 GroupName = Group->getName(); 0
1234 Flags |= ELF::SHF_GROUP; 0
1235 } ----
1236 return Ctx->getELFSection(Name, ELF::SHT_PROGBITS, Flags, 0, GroupName, true, 0
1237 ElfSec.getUniqueID(), ----
1238 cast(TextSec->getBeginSymbol())); 0
1239 } ----

30 static bool useCompactUnwind(const Triple &T) { 30 static bool useCompactUnwind(const Triple &T) {
31 // Only on darwin. 31 // Only on darwin.
32 if (!T.isOSDarwin()) 32 if (!T.isOSDarwin())
33 return false; 33 return false;
34 34
35 // aarch64 always has it. 35 // aarch64 always has it.
36 if (T.getArch() == Triple::aarch64 || T.getArch() == Triple::aarch64_32) 36 if (T.getArch() == Triple::aarch64 || T.getArch() == Triple::aarch64_32)
37 return true; 37 return true;
38 38
39 // armv7k always has it. 39 // armv7k always has it.
40 if (T.isWatchABI()) 40 if (T.isWatchABI())
41 return true; 41 return true;
42 42
43 // Use it on newer version of OS X. 43 // Use it on newer version of OS X.
44 if (T.isMacOSX() && !T.isMacOSXVersionLT(10, 6)) 44 if (T.isMacOSX() && !T.isMacOSXVersionLT(10, 6))
45 return true; 45 return true;
46 46
47 // And the iOS simulator. 47 // And the iOS simulator.
48 if (T.isiOS() && T.isX86()) 48 if (T.isiOS() && T.isX86())
49 return true; 49 return true;
50 50
51 // The rest of the simulators always have it. 51 // The rest of the simulators always have it.
52 if (T.isSimulatorEnvironment()) 52 if (T.isSimulatorEnvironment())
53 return true; 53 return true;
54 54
55 return false; 55 return false;
56 } 56 }
